<Time>1488585904073</Time><user_name>Leila Moshref-Danesh<//user_name>< Pictures>

<response>None< /response><gmap_id>0x80dcb1b0043168c7:0xd3cdadc48d3a6ee0<//gmap_id>< user_id>
106264509773220096368<//user_id>
< review>
1st time customer, made same day appt. i was told id have to put a credit card down. No mention of a cancellation policy. Full disclosure, I was 6 minutes late.  Was called at three minutes late and tersely informed that my appt was being bumped. Not a big deal to be bumped. Rudeness is a big deal. Got there and sat waiting, had a chance to then read their policies.

The store policies are written in an insulting manner. They refer to customers that are even a few minutes late as "flakes", "flakaroonies", and "cornflakes." They specifically state that if you are a flake you probably shouldn't make an appointment with them, that they "don't like flakey people." According to their definition, I was a "flake" and they did not like me. I felt very insulted by this policy. I allotted an appropriate amount of time to travel, but did not realize they were located across train tracks and did not account for being stuck at a train. I didn't mind being bumped as the appointments are very short, but I did not appreciate being labeled by them. I certainly no longer felt comfortable to allow them to wax the most sensitive areas of my body!

I approached the counter and asked to please cancel my appointment, that I no longer felt comfortable. The individual at the counter (the same person who ran my card, it turned out) told me she was sorry I was uncomfortable but could not refund my money. I asked why. She said because I had not canceled 48 hours prior to my appointment. I had made the appointment that same day, literally 2.5 hours prior. There is no way I could have cancelled. She said she would call her manager and then call me later to let me know whether I could have my money back. She said that she could not issue a refund but her manager could. I said this was not acceptable. I asked to speak to the manager. She said I would have to wait about 20 minutes, but could not give me a specific time. I was about to give up in frustration.

The manager, Demi, arrived within about 10 minutes. She was not sympathetic to me not wanting to go through with the service. She made sure to point out that people traveled from all over to have services done. I explained that I did not care about these other people. That I would please like my money back, that as a "flake" I would never bother them by making an appointment there again. She refused. She stated that she had no authority to issue refunds and that I needed to have cancelled 48 hours prior. Again, I do not understand how I could have done that. She said well that's our company policy, which was sent to you in an email. I explained that the email had been sent AFTER they ran my credit card.

Another customer walked in at that point and I could tell the manager did not want them to hear our exchange. She asked me to leave because I was "badgering them". I said I would be happy to leave once I received my refund. The manager refused, saying it would take at least a business day to hear back from corporate. < Text>
I've been living at Fusion for the last 6 months and it's been a great experience so far! TLDR: fairly new luxury building + rooftop pool was a big selling point for me and the new staff took over early 2020 so the older reviews may not reflect the current living conditions.

Pros:
- Beautiful amenities that are well maintained (rooftop pool views, grill areas, clubhouse, gym, kids play area, koi pond)
- Attentive, responsive, and friendly management staff (especially Nelly from the Leasing office and Joe Joe / Daniel from Maintenance)
- Newish property (stainless steel appliances, quartz countertops, hardwood floors in main areas, balcony, parking usually on the same floor as unit, minimal noise level from neighbors)
- Convenient location to highways and shopping areas (Costco/Target/supermarkets; walkable to Diamond Jamboree)

Cons:
- Package delivery to the mailroom can be a nightmare with boxes all over the place, making it difficult to locate your packages. There's a locker system (parcel pending) for safety, but lately it hasn't been used and yet it's a $6 monthly charge.
- Guest parking is limited and sometimes spots run out (so people need to find parking off property). Side note: parking garage is tight when turning; at times it can feel unsafe when cars drive too fast or don't use mirrors to watch for others. Oftentimes there are issues with the garage door entrance/exit as well.
- Outdoor noise level from garbage dumpster, landscaping, or dog park from Fusion or nearby properties (but that's typical for any community).

Overall, I am really enjoying my stay at Fusion. It has everything I'm looking for in a building from a luxury/safety standpoint (rent $ is definitely on the higher end, so I'm not sure if I will renewing my lease). Also before you move in, be sure to download the Rentgrata app to chat with current residents for a possible concession bonus towards your rent (and for whoever refers you). Feel free to reach out directly with any questions! :-)<//Text>

<text>Nuh-uh. Not this Starbucks. I'm sorry, but just, NOPE.

I was so excited when it first opened up. The other Starbucks was half hour walk away. When you have no car to drive, and when you love Starbucks as much as me, you'll understand how excited I was.

However, the drinks were just awful! Maybe it's because the staffs are all new? First, they gave me extra ice when I asked for light ice. I asked them to change it, but they just scooped out all the ice, and left the rest of the cup empty. They offered an explanation before I could point out the empty space. "Sorry, if I add more milk, it'll taste bad." Okay, fine, I'll just drink my half cup of mocha when I payed for the price of one.

Few days later, a friend asked me to bring her a cup of latte macchiato. I also got myself a cup of the mango dragonfruit drink. When she got her drink, it just tasted like heavy creamer and milk. There was absolutely no flavor in it other wise. Sadly, we had to throw the whole cup away. I drank my mango dragonfruit, but it was very watered down, and I think they forgot about the mango syrup...

Few months later (a week or two weeks ago), I thought they had enough time to learn, so I went and visited again. I got myself a cup of white chocolate mocha. Ugh... It looked just like milk (yes, pain white), and taste just like milk.... I asked the server about it, and she kindly remade my drink. "With extra pump of white mocha," she says. Only, this time it was so sweet, the mocha and chocolate flavor was way too much. Well, it's better than the milk...

It's going to be another few months before I come back. Hopefully, they'll be real Starbucks by then... Hopefully...< /text>< Gmap_id>

<UserId.>102275310503004124389<//UserId.><gmapID>0x80c32f162a7b861f:0xfb5506056b5f6617</gmapID>< Pictures>
[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPWFzwkc5aT_iMvMe0xQNgrHPGEdOW_rpz0_Tqo=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pictures>

< Review>
Since taking a trip to Italy last year, this is hands down our favorite Italian restaurant in the states. We travel for a living, so we basically eat our way around the world. When Yelpers said to come to this little place just 5 minutes from where we were staying in San Dimas, we were a bit skeptical, but, Yelpers are always right!

This is Italian to the Nth degree. This is NOT fast food. There are like 3 entire people employed here. It's all fresh made, so relax, get some wine and chill out while they make you some food to remember!

We've now been here twice, and have also ordered delivery from Uber Eats. My hands down fav every time is the Chicken Tequila!!! The Chef/Owner (who is the sweetest thing ever) recommended it on our first visit and he basically insisted, so I ordered it. He asked if I like spicy. That's not normally a question you get at an Italian restaurant. I responded that I sure do. He asked "How hot?" I said "7 out of 10?" Well, apparently this fella makes his own hot sauce! He doctored up my Chicken Tequila and DAYUM it was GOOOOOD! I've since gottent hat dish 2 more times. Can't get away from it now. I crave it non stop.

The BF has gotten the Sausage and Peppers (a fav). Veal Marsala (was "bleeping amazing") and then Veal Parm. I also got the Shrimp Bistro once, which was good, but no Chicken Tequila!

Also, the first time we went, we ordered their wine, but then we learned you can BRING YOUR OWN! They'll cork it for $9.99. Awesome!

All in all, we won't be back to CA for 8 months, but I can already SMELL that Chicken Tequila!!<//Review>

I recommend drinking beer instead,  as it will come in a bottle and remove Chandara from the entire equation. You will also appreciate the alcohol as your outing at this awful restaurant continues.

The drinks are creative, delicious, and beautiful. The short rib sandwich is flavorful and tender. I ordered it with fries.  The fries were a very generous portion. Menu is on a QR code so bring your charged mobile device. I had a problem with my signal and it took a really long time to load the menu. It would be nice if they posted the menu in the window so people could take a picture of it if they can't download it. I appreciated the heat lamps for outdoor seating.</Text>

< name>
Juan Miguel Silva< /name>
< review>
Imagine biting into a caramel covered apple only to discover that it is actually an onion.

Overpriced cafeteria food.

The place has a nice and laid back ambience that lulls you into believing that you are in for a gastronomically satisfying experience.

There is a marked gap between the price of the menu items and what actually arrives in front of you.

To be fair, the Brussel sprouts were good, albeit slightly over cooked.

The entree's are a different story. If you were out for dinner to satisfy your hunger, you will be gravely disappointed.
You would literally have better food out of a vending machine.

I recommend having an actual meal before eating here so that the disappointing food would be less of a heartbreak once it touches your poor unsuspecting tastebuds.

The drinks were good but the alcohol was not enough to mask the unfortunate tasting food.

If you want good food, go elsewhere.

If you want to get drunk in a pretentious ambiance, this is the place to be.

It's better off marketed as a bar that serves food, that way you know up front that it's a place to drink, not to eat at.< /review>

< Text>
They've succeeded in making a hip bar/restaurant in the Outer Richmond, but the service is lacking, the food is overpriced, and it's really cramped.

We showed up on time for a 7:30 reservation and were in line to check in. Just as we were about to check in, a woman pushed past us and asked to be seated. The host stand is in a really unfortunate place, so perhaps she didn't notice that we were standing in line. We were seated right after, so it didn't seem like a big deal. BUT... after being seated, it took another 15-20 minutes for us to even be greeted by a waiter. It was so long, in fact, that the woman who'd cut us in line had already received appetizers by the time someone took our drink order. I had to get up and talk to the manager to get anyone's attention.

The place is also really small, and it definitely feels like they packed in at least one too many tables. I'd suggest that they need another waiter for that many tables, but there's really no room. It's also loud. Granted, the loud, packed feel contributes to the "hip" feel of the place, but don't expect to be able to have an intimate conversation here.

The food was fairly good. Oysters seemed fresh and well selected. Had an Impossible Burger (really glad they have this option, actually!) and shared a salad. For a half dozen oysters, one salad, two burgers, and no drinks: $90 after tax and tip. Not insane for SF, but definitely overpriced.< /Text>

< Text>
A friend took me here when I was visiting SF, after I arrived late and this restaurant was new and within walking distance.

The first thing I noticed was the lack of variety on the menu. It seemed like everything was either tiny appetizer portions, or huge entrees.... nothing in between. We ordered our drinks.... the Pear thee Well and an Old Fashioned, and shared the grilled artichokes, and two salads.... my friend got the caesar salad with shrimp, and I ordered the seasonal winter salad that I forgot the name of. When I was deciding between items, I told the server that I wanted the salad instead of the Devils on Horseback (dates, bacon and blue cheese). He sent them out anyway, but oh well.

Both salads were okay but wayyyyy overdressed. I couldn't finish mine. Everything else was just okay. I've had better bacon-wrapped dates and this only came with 3. When I asked whether the Pear thee Well was sweet, our server (who wasn't the friendliest) told me flatly "it's balanced." It was overpoweringly sweet and tasted like it was mostly sour mix... I couldn't taste anything else.... no pear flavor or alcohol. I ended up sending it back for an old fashioned, which was the best item I had there.

When our server brought the check, we asked for one more round of drinks. Our server told us that the kitchen was closing, but we could go to the bar and order more drinks (which was a few feet away from us). It didn't seem to make sense, because he totally could have placed the order and had us check out separately with the bar, or just add another round of drinks to the check before he brought it (more tip for him, right?). They seemed to be using the same POS system. It wasn't the level of service you'd think you'd get for how much we paid for the food (after paying $8 for 3 dates, I'd at least hope for a "I'm sorry, I have to close the check with you, but let me just ask the bar to start working on those for you.") We didn't feel welcome and ended up going home for more drinks.<//Text>
